The extension finds images on web pages that do not have any \"alt text\", i.e., captions provided for the image by the web page author. When it finds such an image, it sends the image's source (i.e., URL) to a web service. That web service uses the Bing Image Search API to request both a caption and known web pages containing the same image (or related image).
